> 4130:"A sorcery fit for only the masters of the craft. This effect stacks up to nine times. \nWhen you cast your tenth Glint Sorcery, all previous stacks are canceled and you gain a buff for 30 seconds. \nThat buff increases the damage of all Glint Sorceries by 15%, reduces the FP cost of sorceries by 20%, grants 20 FP regeneration per second and you gain additional poise. \nWhile this effect is active, you cannot gain stacks.\n\nThis spell is in essence the perfected form of what both Master Lusat and Master Azur were pursuing, a pure infusion of glintstone into the body and therefore a method of channeling the primeval current directly into sorceries. \nWhile the old masters' efforts ultimately fell short, such a technique would never be possible without their sacrifice.\n"

= 4852:"“亵渎君王”拉卡德的魔法。\n传说中的法术\n获得一个效果，每次敌人死亡时额外提升1%血量, 专注值和精力以及1%额外伤害，此技能最多可叠加10次。\n效果永不过期，重放该法术以开关该效果。\n\n拉卡德为了获得与黄金树相抗衡的力量，他牺牲自己的人性，让自己被大蛇吞噬。在他看来，这不是一种牺牲，而是通往神国的垫脚石。在这种形态下，他希望既能运用蛇的力量，又能融合他所吞噬的所有灵魂的力量。然而，他没有预见到的是，他自己至高无上的欲望被蛇吞噬一切的欲望所取代。因此，他的身心完全迷失了。"

= 4860:"古代的艾格蕾崇拜的一种魔法。\n\n在脚下释放一个巨大的熔岩池，对接触到的任何敌人造成伤害。\n\n对艾格蕾的崇拜发现了熔岩的许多用途，而这些都是拉卡德在他对权力的痴迷追求中所回避的。"
> 4861:"A sorcery made in error by the ancient cult of Eiglay.\n\nCauses the caster to conjure pools of lava underneath their feet, causing damage to any enemy that steps on them. The effect lasts 30 seconds.\n\nIt behooved the first sorcerers of the great volcano to create a means of travel over the great molten lakes and rivers that barred their path to their benefactor, the great serpent. This spell was the result of a failed attempt in that effort."
= 4861:"一种由古老的艾格蕾教派制造的错误魔法。\n\n在施法者脚下释放熔岩池，对任何踩到他们的敌人造成伤害。效果持续30秒。\n\n火山的第一批巫师理所当然地创造了一种穿越巨大的熔岩湖泊和河流的工具，这些湖泊和河流挡住了他们通往恩人——大蛇的道路。这个魔法是一次失败的尝试的结果。"
> 4870:"A sorcery of the cult of Eiglay, fit only for masters of magma manipulation.\n\nFire a seething mass of lava at enemies that explodes on impact.\n\nOne of the lost techniques of the ancient cult. Such secrets were never disseminated to the acolytes for fear that they might usurp the authority of the elders in a coup."
= 4870:"艾格蕾崇拜的魔法，只适合操纵岩浆的大师。\n\n向敌人发射一团沸腾的熔岩，并在击中时爆炸。\n\n这是古代异教中失传的招式之一。这些秘密从来没有泄露给助手，因为担心他们可能会在政变中篡夺长老的权威。"

The lord granted them an audience, whereupon they were welcomed by the maw of the great serpent -- and within the serpent's bowels, they became the lord's kin."

Can be cast multiple times.\n\nThe Albinaurics that inhabit the region around Mohg’s palace have been dwelling in the corrupted blood of the sacrificed for a prolonged time. > 4911:"An aberrant sorcery of those branded as guilty.\n\nWhen this spell is cast, it causes bleed buildup on you.\n\nSend trails of bloodthorns in all directions around you that impale enemies from below, dealing damage and building bleed.\n\nA consequence of glintstone corruption is that the source of the magic is no longer drawn from the stars but from the natural world and from the body of the sorcerer themselves. The Blood Star resides not in the cosmos but within all those that carry darkness within.\n"
= 4911:"有罪之人的异端魔法。\n\n当这个魔法被施放时，它会在你身上造成流血。\n\n向周围的各个方向发射血刺之痕，从下面刺穿敌人，造成伤害并造成流血。\n\n辉石腐败的一个后果是魔法的来源不再来自星星，而是来自自然世界和巫师自己的身体。鲜血星星并不存在于宇宙中，而是存在于所有携带黑暗的人之中。"

= 5011:"侍奉死亡的人物施展的魔法。\n\n召唤一群复仇的灵魂，追逐敌人，造成圣属性伤害。蓄力增强威力。\n\n它们是远古死亡魔法的灰烬，由死之鸟从灵火中挖出。"
> 5012:"A sorcery inspired by the funerary rites of the Deathbirds.\n\nStrike your staff into the ground to conjure a series of ghostflame explosions around you, dealing holy damage. Hold to increase duration.\n\nWhile the act of heralding souls was not a benign process, the deathbirds did not perform them for the purpose of waging war, as that was not their nature. \nNecromancers have no such scruples.\n"
= 5012:"受死亡仪式鸟启发的魔法。\n\n将杖击向地面，在周围召唤一系列灵火爆炸。按住可以增加持续时间，造成圣属性伤害。蓄力增加持续时间。\n\n虽然预告灵魂的行为并非善意，但死之鸟没有以发动战争为目的，因为这不是它们的本性。\n死灵法师则没有这样的顾虑。"
< 5020:"Sorcery of Fia, the Deathbed Companion.\n\nCreates a deathly mist before the caster, which inflicts Death blight upon those who enter.\nThis sorcery can be cast while in motion. Charging enhances range of the mist.\n\nThis sorcery was developed to oppose the Roundtable Hold, and is effective only against the Tarnished."
> 5020:"Sorcery of Fia, the Deathbed Companion.\n\nCreates a deathly mist before the caster, which inflicts holy damage and Death blight upon those who enter. \nThis sorcery can be cast while in motion. Charging enhances range of the mist.\n\nThis sorcery was developed to oppose the Roundtable Hold."

On impact, it curses the enemy causing constant build-up of Death Blight for 30 seconds.\n\nThis sorcery was derived from the bodies of those consumed by the corruption of blight that has taken root throughout the Lands Between.\n"
= 5021:"一种由异端死灵法师施行的魔法。\n\n向敌人发射枯萎的飞弹，并在命中时诅咒敌人，造成持续30秒的死亡枯萎。\n\n这种魔法来自于那些被腐败的枯萎病吞噬的人的尸体，这种腐败病已经在大地之间扎根。"
> 5022:"A curse that strikes at the frailty of flesh, accelerating decay.\n\nSends out a projectile toward foes which, upon impact, curses the enemy. \nThe curse lowers the target’s absorption to holy damage by 10% and deals holy damage over time. Lasts for 20 seconds.\n\nThe deathbed companions have made a study of decay, only a very few would seek to put their knowledge into such a maligned form.\n"
= 5022:"一个攻击脆弱肉体，加速腐败的诅咒。\n\n向敌人发射飞弹，击中可诅咒敌人人。\n诅咒降低目标10%圣属性减伤率，并持续造成圣属性伤害。持续20秒。\n\n临终的同伴们已经研究了腐败，只有极少数人会试图把他们的知识变成这样一种恶意的形式。"
> 5023:"A sorcery made in tribute to the Prince of Death and his insidious legacy.\n\nSlam your staff into the ground causing an explosion of deathblight to slowly spread out on the ground in front of you, causing holy damage and building Death blight to any enemy it touches.\n\nAfter Godwyn's murder and the spread of his corruption, many sorcerers' doubt in the Erdtree and Golden Order's divine right was justified. Powers beyond the Greater Will existed. Sorceries of this nature became seen as cathartic revelries and were adopted by the first necromancers.\n"
= 5023:"这是一种向死王子和他恶意遗产致敬的魔法。\n\n将杖猛击地面，造成死亡枯萎的爆炸，在面前的地面上慢慢扩散，造成圣属性伤害，并对任何它接触到的敌人造成死亡枯萎。\n\n在葛德文被谋杀且腐败开始扩散之后，巫师们发现，他们对黄金树和黄金律法的神圣权利的质疑变得正当起来。\n确实存在着无上意志之外的力量。\n这种性质的魔法被看作是宣泄的狂欢，并为第一批死灵魔法师们采纳。"
> 5050:"A sorcery inspired by the funerary rites of the Deathbirds.\n\nInstantly kill your summoned minions. When they die, you recover all HP, FP and stamina points. \nYou also receive a buff that increases your absorption and holy damage you deal by 10% for 30 seconds.\n\nThe inversion of ghostflame retains the transient power of dissipating spirits. \nRather than releasing the energy in the form of rancor or cold flame, the power is diverted to the ritualist. \nSuch a thing would be considered an abomination to the followers of the great phoenix as it prevents the eventual rebirth of those souls.\n"
= 5050:"受死亡仪式鸟启发的魔法。\n\n立即杀死你召唤的随从。当他们死亡时，你会恢复所有血量, 专注值和精力。\n你还会得到一个buff，使你的减伤率和圣属性攻击力提高10%，持续30秒。\n\n灵火的反转保留了驱散灵魂的短暂力量。\n而不是以怨恨或冰冷火焰的形式释放能量，力量被转移到仪式的人。\n对于伟大凤凰的追随者来说，这样的事情将被认为是令人憎恶的，因为它阻止了那些灵魂的最终重生。"
> 5060:"A sorcery inspired by the funerary rites of the Deathbirds.\n\nEnvelop the caster, all allies and summons in ghostflame. Any nearby enemy will take holy damage and frostbite build-up. \nWhen someone affected by Ghostflame Embrace dies, it causes a large ghostflame explosion, dealing holy damage and causing frost build-up.\nLasts 40 seconds.\n\nA small portion of the funeral ritual of the Deathbirds, this sorcery has been repurposed by many heretical necromancers, turning them and their wayward spirits into walking weapons.\n"
= 5060:"受死亡仪式鸟启发的魔法。\n\n将施法者、所有盟友和召唤物包围在灵火中。任何附近的敌人将受到圣属性伤害和累积冻伤。\n当受灵火拥抱影响的人死亡时，会引发一个巨大的灵火爆炸，造成圣属性伤害并造成累积冻伤。\n持续40秒。\n\n作为死亡仪式鸟的小众群体，这种魔法被许多异端的死灵法师重新利用，把他们和他们任性的灵魂变成了行走的武器。"
> 5061:"Sorcery of the servants of Death.\n\nViolently rip an enemy’s soul from their body as a projectile that moves toward the caster. The enemy instantly becomes stunned. \nWhen the soul is absorbed, the caster becomes drained of all stamina for a few seconds and loses all remaining FP. \n\nIf the caster is affected by the Phoenix of Death sorcery, this spell will replenish the Death Ward effect of that spell if Death Ward is not currently active.\n"
= 5061:"侍奉死亡的人物施展的魔法。\n\n猛烈地将敌人的灵魂从他们的身体中撕裂出来，并以飞弹的形式向施法者移动。敌人立即被击晕。\n当灵魂被吸收时，施法者在几秒钟内耗尽所有精力，并失去所有剩余的专注值。\n\n如果施法者受到死之凤凰魔法的影响，该法术将在死亡之盾失效的情况下补充该法术的死亡之盾效果。"

= 5080:"一种由异端死灵法师施行的魔法。\n永久性法术\n使施法者免疫精神召唤减益并提升8点精力恢复。\n这个魔法不会过期。再次施法以开关效果。\n\n对于死灵法师来说，牺牲自己的一小部分灵魂来找到与他们召唤的仆从更好的亲和力是一种常见的做法。\n随着时间的推移，这种对不死状态的调谐会给他们带来损失，有些人认为最终会导致他们自己变得失魂。"

> 5221:"An advanced sorcery used by the Tempestcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nCall down a large funnel of wind centered around your body that moves with you. Enemies in a large area around you will take continuous damage for the duration. \nLasts for 30 seconds.\n\nThe greatest of storm techniques could only be employed by an elite few. \nThese masters of the art were eventually honored with the title of Tempestcallers, a moniker that would ultimately make them targets of assassination by Queen Marika's minions. \n\n\n\n"
= 5221:"古代史东薇尔的召唤者使用的高级魔法。\n\n释放一个旋风，围绕着身体，和你一起移动。你周围大范围内的敌人将持续受到伤害。\n持续30秒。\n\n最伟大的风暴招式只能由少数精英使用。\n这些招式大师最终被授予风暴使者的称号，这一称号最终使他们成为玛莉卡女王的仆从暗杀的目标。"
> 5222:"An advanced sorcery used by the Tempestcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nConjure a large funnel of wind that moves toward foes and brings destruction to all it touches. Only one tornado can be conjured at a time. \nLasts 8 seconds.\n\nOne of the Tempestcallers' greatest achievements, techniques like this were daunting on the battlefield. Realizing martial victory was unlikely, Marika's commanders ultimately employed methods of subterfuge and sabotage to defeat Stormveil.\n"
= 5222:"古代史东薇尔的召唤者使用的高级魔法。\n\n召唤一个巨大的漏斗状旋风，向敌人移动，并给它所接触的一切带来毁灭。一次只能召唤出一个龙卷风。\n持续8秒。\n\n风暴使者最伟大的成就之一，像这样的招式力量在战场上令人望而生畏。\n当通过军事手段取得胜利的可能性变得渺茫时，玛莉卡的指挥官最终动用诡计和破坏手段击溃了史东薇尔。"
> 5230:"A sorcery used by the Stormcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nConjure a continuous cylinder of air in front of you. The spell strikes enemies multiple times dealing damage. This spell deals exceptional posture damage. Charging increases duration.\n\nA spell created for the purpose of immobilizing foes on the battlefield, bombarding them with buffeting winds and neutralizing them as a threat. \n\n\n\n"
= 5230:"古代史东薇尔的风暴使者使用的魔法。\n\n在你面前释放一系列连续的柱装旋风。该法术对敌人造成多次伤害。该法术造成特殊的姿势伤害。蓄力增加持续时间。\n\n这是一种法术，用于使战场上的敌人无法动弹，用猛烈的风轰炸他们，并使他们失去威胁。"
> 5240:"A sorcery of the knights of old Stormveil.\n\nSlash horizontally into the air with your staff, generating a slender blade of air that flies forward, slicing through enemies.\n\nAccidentally discovered by the now banished retainers of Stormhill, this sorcery at first brought shame to their order, as it was seen as dishonorable to engage with enemies from afar. \nThey likened such tactics to cowardice and trickery.\n\n\n"
= 5240:"旧史东薇尔骑士的魔法。\n\n用杖向空中水平斩击，产生一个向前飞的细长气刃，切割敌人。\n\n现在被放逐的风暴山丘的守卫们偶然发现了这一魔法，一开始他们感到羞耻，因为偷袭远方的敌人被认为是不光彩的。\n他们把这种策略比作怯懦和欺骗。"
> 5241:"A sorcery used by the Stormcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nCall down a small torrent of air upon foes, dealing damage.\n\nThe namesake of the school, this sorcery was among the first to be employed in the long fallen kingdom of Stormveil. \nSome believe that the endless prevailing wind of the region was an inspiration for the craft and others say it was caused by the stormcaller's elemental meddling. \nIt is a secret now lost to the ages. \n\n\n\n"
= 5241:"古代史东薇尔的风暴使者使用的魔法。\n\n向敌人释放一股气流，造成伤害。\n\n与这所学校同名的魔法，是最早在衰落已久的史东薇尔王国使用的魔法之一。\n一些人认为，该地区无尽的盛行风是飞船的灵感来源，而另一些人则认为这是由风暴使者的元素干预造成的。\n这是一个随着时代的流逝而消失的秘密。"
> 5242:"An advanced sorcery used by the Tempestcallers of ancient Stormveil.\n\nFire a projectile of air at foes that causes moderate damage but massive damage to their posture.\n\nTempestcallers learned over time that precision counts for as much as strength on the battlefield. \nVery few practitioners could boast the control required to use such a sorcery.\n\n\n\n"
= 5242:"古代史东薇尔的召唤者使用的高级魔法。\n\n向敌人发射气体飞弹，造成中等伤害，但对其姿势造成巨大伤害。\n\n随着时间的推移，风暴使者明白了在战场上精确度和力量一样重要。\n很少有人能够夸耀使用这种魔法所需要的控制能力。"
> 5250:"A sorcery used by the Stormcallers of ancient Stormveil.\nWeapon Enchantment\nEnchants armaments held in the right hand with physical-affinity attacks.\nThis sorcery can be cast while in motion.\n\nThe knights of old Stormveil would often employ these techniques in battle, as a devotion to elemental forces was compulsory for any member of their creed. \nA devotion that would see most them banished as heretics in time.\n \n\n"
= 5250:"古代史东薇尔的风暴使者使用的魔法。\n附魔的法术\n强化右手的武器，附加物理属性攻击力。\n这个魔法可以在移动中施放。\n\n旧史东薇尔的骑士们经常在战斗中使用这些技巧，因为效忠于元素力量对他们信仰的任何成员都是强制性的。\n这种虔诚让他们中的大多数人最终被视为异教徒而被驱逐。"
> 5260:"An enchantment employed by the elders of Stormveil Castle.\nSignature Enchantment\nInfuse your body with the essence of air, causing the caster to automatically sprint with no stamina use, also dramatically increases stamina recovery, increases casting speed by 40 and prevents fall damage. \nLasts for 1 minute.\n\nOne of the earliest stable iterations of air infusions that affect the sorcerer’s body. Earlier versions of such practices were dangerous as failed attempts could lead to vaporization.\n\n \n\n"
= 5260:"史东薇尔城长老使用的魔法。\n标志性法术\n给身体注入风的精华，使施法者在不使用精力的情况下自动冲刺，也显著提升精力恢复，提升40点施法速度，并防止坠落伤害。\n持续1分钟。\n\n最早的稳定风能注入，影响巫师的身体。这种做法在早期是危险的，因为失败的尝试可能导致蒸发。"
> 5261:"An enchantment employed by the elders of Stormveil Castle.\nDefensive Enchantment\nAlter the essence of your physical form into vapors causing the stamina cost of attacks to be decreased by 25%, the FP cost of sorceries to be decreased by 15% and your physical absorption to be increased by 25%. \nLasts for 2 minutes.\n\nA derivative of the Cloud Form enchantment, this technique became invaluable in the great conflict against the force of the Erdtree. \n\n \n\n"
= 5261:"史东薇尔城长老使用的魔法。\n防御性法术\n将自身物质形态的本质转化为气态，降低25%攻击精力消耗、15%魔法专注值消耗，提升25%物理减伤率。\n持续2分钟。\n\n作为气态魔法的衍生物，这项招式在对抗黄金树之力的巨大冲突中价值连城。"

Upon impact, the enemy will be affected by a curse that greatly inhibits their breathing. \nDeals continuous damage over its duration, causes affected enemies to deal 15% less damage, lowers their ability to block attacks and lowers their posture. \nLasts for 80 seconds.\n\nMasters of attrition warfare, the knights of old Stormveil stood as bastions on the battlefield, employing spells that could bring enemy troops to the point of exhaustion even before the battle was joined.\n\n \n\n"

< 246000:"Ashen remains in which spirits yet dwell.\nUse to summon the spirits of three little living jars.\nSummoning consumes HP rather than FP.\n\nThese reckless spirits sacrifice themselves to vanquish their summoner's foes, and explode upon death.\nThough their bravery is admirable, their explosions can harm friend as well as foe, and they will also immediately explode on contact with fire.\n\n\"Tell the others—tell them how brightly a fire jar burns.\""

- 246002:"寄宿着灵魂的骨灰。\n能召唤３名小型活壶的灵魂。\n召唤时不消耗专注值，而是血量。\n\n会对敌人展开特攻，死亡时会爆炸，\n一群视死如归的灵魂。\n表现得很勇敢，但爆炸也会波及我方。\n碰触到火焰会立刻爆炸。\n\n\u3000帮我们转告给故乡的大家吧──\n\u3000我们火焰壶，表现的点点滴滴……"
